country_event = {
	id = iran_md.1 # Flag change (alt hist)
	title = iran_md.1.t
	desc = iran_md.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_civil_war
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = iran_md.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.1.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					PER = {
						nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				PER = { set_cosmetic_tag = PER_AUTH_PAN }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = divide_turkey.2 # Iran Wants Us To Embargo Turkey for armenia
	title = divide_turkey.2.t
	desc = divide_turkey.2.d
	picture = GFX_TUR_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o1 executed"
		SOV = {
			send_embargo = TUR
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		PER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = development_plan.1 # The Third Development Plan
	title = development_plan.1.t
	desc = development_plan.1.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Industry
		name = development_plan.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o1 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = industry_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_industry
	}
	option = { # Science
		name = development_plan.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o2 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = science_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_science
	}
	option = { # Military
		name = development_plan.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o3 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = military_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_military
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reorganize_school.1
	title = reorganize_school.t
	desc = reorganize_school.d
	picture = GFX_school_reorganize
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.a
		log = "l"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_3
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_4
		}
	}
}

	title = PER_contact_k.2.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.2.desc
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #offer money
		name = PER_contact_k.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_k.2.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = PER

				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			country_event = {

				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.6 # Deal goes through
	title = PER_contact_k.6.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.6.d
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept tech
		name = PER_contact_k.6.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_tech_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 2
					category = industry
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_resource_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				create_import = {
					resource = oil
					amount = 16
					exporter = PER
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_moni_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			PER = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.7 # Iran goes to NK
	title = PER_contact_k.7.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.7.d
	picture = GFX_hung_2020
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #contact NK
		name = PER_contact_k.7.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
			}
			country_exists = NKO
		}
		NKO = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_nk.1
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No one else
		name = PER_contact_k.7.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = NKO
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_1
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.7.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
	}
}

		}

				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_tech_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.15
						uses = 2
						category = industry
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_resource_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					create_import = {
						resource = oil
						amount = 16
						exporter = PER
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_moni_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
				PER = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_nk.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_NKO_nd_2
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = PER_contact_with_countries.36.o1 # It's time to change...

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		add_popularity = { # Increase Emerging
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = communism
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PER
						modifier = no_diplomatic_ties
					}

							target = TUR
							modifier = no_diplomatic_ties
						}

					}
					SOV = {
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					ARM = {
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					TUR = {
						NATO_leave = yes
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } }
							hidden_effect = {
								clear_array = ruling_party
								clear_array = gov_coalition_array
								add_to_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
								update_government_coalition_strength = yes
								update_party_name = yes

								set_ruling_leader = yes
								set_leader = yes
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 50 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = USA }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = GER }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ENG }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
					}
				}
			}
			60 = {
				hidden_effect = {
					NATO_leave = yes
					set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
					set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 1.00 }
					add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {

							ruling_party = communism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
						set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
						add_relative_party_popularity = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
						set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
						set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
						add_relative_party_popularity = yes
					}

					set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ENG }
					set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }

	id = PER_contact_with_countries.52 # Iran asks Iraq
	title = PER_contact_with_countries.52.t
	desc = PER_contact_with_countries.52.d
	picture = GFX_politics_negotiations
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = PER_contact_with_countries.52.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_with_countries.52.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_half_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_half_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_half_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_half_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_one_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_one_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_two_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_two_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly
		}
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.54 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_iran_attack_iraq_wargoal_TT
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.53 } } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Turkey accepts
	id = PER_orupa.2
	title = PER_orupa.2.t
	desc = PER_orupa.2.d
	picture = GFX_orupa

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
	name = PER_orupa.2.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_orupa.2.a executed"
	set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.16 }
	modify_treasury_effect = yes
		build_railway = {
		  level = 1
		  path = { 9893 3899 11746 11810 9830 9763 9755 940 11860 9878 3983 3951 3786 11811 11829 9833 }
		  start_province = 9893
		  target_province = 9833
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				add_ideas = { PER_TUR_shia_influence }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
				add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
						emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		GRE = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	name = PER_orupa.2.b
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_orupa.2.b executed"
	}
}

					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}
				NOT = {
					GER = { has_country_flag = PER_mediation_refused }
					FRA = { has_country_flag = PER_mediation_refused }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = PER_nuclear_compromise.14 days = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						GER = { has_country_flag = PER_mediation_refused }
						FRA = { has_country_flag = PER_mediation_refused }
					}
					AND = {
						GER = { has_country_flag = GER_mediation_support }
						ENG = { has_country_flag = PER_mediation_refused }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = PER_nuclear_compromise.15 days = 0 }
		}
		else = { country_event = { id = PER_nuclear_compromise.4 days = 0 } }
	}
}
country_event = { #if enough majors, continues
	id = PER_nuclear_compromise.14
	title = PER_nuclear_compromise.14.t
	desc = PER_nuclear_compromise.14.d
	picture = GFX_hung_2020

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #supports
	name = PER_nuclear_compromise.14.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_nuclear_compromise.14.a executed"
	set_country_flag = PER_enough_majors
		PER = {
		complete_national_focus = PER_negotiate_a_compromise
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Iran gets sanctions
	id = PER_sanctions_event.1
	title = PER_sanctions_event.1.t
	desc = PER_sanctions_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_iran_sanctions

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #dam
	name = PER_sanctions_event.1.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_sanctions_event.1.a executed"
	unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_resistance_economy
	add_ideas = { PER_economic_sanctions }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PER_resistance_econ
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = GER_mediation_support
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = PER_sanctions_event.2
						days = 100
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:axis_of_resistance_events.1.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		PER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		news_event = {
			id = axis_of_resistance_events.3
			days = 0
		}
		PER = {
			clr_country_flag = invited_syria
			clr_country_flag = invited_iraq
			clr_country_flag = invited_houthis
			clr_country_flag = invited_hezbollah
			clr_country_flag = invited_azerbaijan
			clr_country_flag = invited_turkey
		}
	}
	option = { # No.
		name = axis_of_resistance_events.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:axis_of_resistance_events.1.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = -1
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = axis_of_resistance_events.2
				days = 0
			}

		}
	}

		}

		}

### Iranian Presidental Elections Events ###

country_event = { # Event to automatically choose presidents based on popularity and date
	id = PER_election_events.1
	title = PER_election_events.1.t
	desc = PER_election_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_election
	trigger = {
		tag = PER
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		}
		OR = {
			date > 2001.2.1
			date > 2005.2.1
			date > 2009.2.1
			date > 2013.2.1
			date > 2017.2.1
			date > 2021.2.1
		}

	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	timeout_days = 1
	immediate = {
		if = { #8th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2001.1.1
					date < 2002.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.2
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #9th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2005.1.1
					date < 2006.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.3
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #10th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2009.1.1
					date < 2010.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #11th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2013.1.1
					date < 2014.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #12th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2017.1.1
					date < 2018.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.6
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #13th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2021.1.1
					date < 2022.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.7
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.1.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}
}

					days = 20
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					30 = { # 30% Chance that Ghalibaf withdraws with historical AI off

						id = PER_election_events.21
						days = 20
					}
					}
					70 = { }
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Khatami Elected as President 2001 (Reformists Won)
	id = PER_election_events.8
	title = PER_election_events.8.t
	desc = PER_election_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_khatami_won_election
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.8.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.8.a executed"

		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes

		set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 8 }
		change_ruling_party_effect = yes

		PER_scripted_effect_finish_election = yes
		set_country_flag = PER_president_khatami # Set President
		add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
		add_ideas = PER_khatami_idea
	}
}

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Sayyid Ali Hosseini Khamenei"
					picture = "sayyid_ali_hosseini_khamenei.dds"

				capital = 402

				}

country_event = { #Meant for player
	id = PER_revolution.15
	title = PER_revolution.15.t
	desc = PER_revolution.15.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_mek_rebellion
	option = { #This is it for them!
		name = PER_revolution.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_revolution.15.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = do_not_retire

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } #Pahlavi
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } #Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } #Communist-State
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } #Moderate Shiite
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } #Hardline Shiite
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } #Caliphate
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } #Kingdom
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } #Neutral_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } #neutral socialist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } #neutral communist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = nationalist
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } #Pan Iranist?
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } #Pan Iranist?
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } #Nat_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } #Monarchist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}

			clr_country_flag = do_not_retire
			clr_country_flag = PER_mojahed_civil_war
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_sway.300.a executed"
		set_power_balance = {
			id = PER_clergy_balance_of_power_category
			set_default = yes
		}
		#
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				create_intelligence_agency = {
					name = "Sazman-e Etela'at"
					icon = GFX_intelligence_agency_logo_generic_5
				}
			}
			increase_economic_growth = yes
			decrease_corruption = yes
			# Iran loses influence
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -20 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = IRQ }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -90 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = HEZ }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -20 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = IRQ }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -20 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = YEM }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -20 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SYR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -20 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SUD }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			#
			country_event = {
				id = PER_revolution.3
				days = 2
			}
			#
			set_country_flag = do_not_retire

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } #Western Autocracy
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } #Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } #Communist-State
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } #Moderate Shiite
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } #Hardline Shiite
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } #Caliphate
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } #Kingdom
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } #Neutral_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } #neutral socialist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } #neutral communist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = nationalist
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } #Nat_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } #Monarchist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } #fascist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}

			clr_country_flag = do_not_retire
		}
		#
		clr_country_flag = PER_civil_war
		clr_country_flag = PER_controlled_majlis
		set_country_flag = PER_freed_majlis
		news_event = {
			id = PER_rev_flavor.8
			days = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IRQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = PER_revolution.5
					days = 720
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = PER_iran_reborn
		clr_country_flag = PER_iranian_civilwar
	}
}

		}

				has_opinion = { target = PER value > 39 }

			}
		}
	}

		}

country_event = { ##Iran wants us to join the Iranic Union
	id = PER_political.2150
	title = PER_political.2150.t
	desc = PER_political.2150.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Sure
		name = PER_political.2150.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.2150.a executed"
		set_country_flag = PER_afghans_in
		AFG = {
			every_core_state = {
				transfer_state_to = PER
			}
		}
		AFG = { every_core_state = { add_core_of = PER } }
		hidden_effect = {
			PER = {
				country_event = {
					id = PER_political.87878
					days = 0
				}
			}
			414 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			412 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			415 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			TAL = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PER
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
			TAL = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Taliban Rebels"
					regiments = {
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					}
					priority = 2
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name =\"Taliban Rebels\" division_template = \"Taliban Rebels\" start_experience_factor =  1.0"
						owner = TAL
						count = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 6
		}
	}
	option = { #No
		name = PER_political.2150.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.2150.b executed"
		AFG = { every_core_state = { add_core_of = PER } }
		PER = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = AFG
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
	}
}

# NOTES # 8/8/2023
#Elections for historical every 4 years. Only Reformist or Principalist can win
#Elections for alt-history every 4 years. Reformist and Principalists cannot win. For Alt-History, add NOT = { X_party_is_in_power = yes } to determine seats lost
#Election outcomes will be mostly random, but a player can hinder the outcome if they decide to allocate funding to their ideologies bloc


### MAJLIS OUTCOMES ###


country_event = { #Reformist Majority elected
	id = PER_majlis.27
	title = PER_majlis.27.t
	desc = PER_majlis.27.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_majlis.27.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.27.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				check_variable = {
					PER_majlis_support < 50
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
			#
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 100
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 150
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -90 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 200
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -110 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -130 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support > 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -150 }
			}
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				check_variable = {
					PER_majlis_support < 50
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 130 }
			#
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 100
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 70 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 150
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 200
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 30 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support > 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 15 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
		clr_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}
#
country_event = { #Principalists Majority elected
	id = PER_majlis.28
	title = PER_majlis.28.t
	desc = PER_majlis.28.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_majlis.28.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.28.a executed"
		#LOSING
		if = {
			limit = {
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				check_variable = {
					PER_majlis_support < 50
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
			#
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 100
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 150
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -90 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 200
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -110 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -130 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support > 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -150 }
			}
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				check_variable = {
					PER_majlis_support < 50
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 130 }
			#
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 100
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 70 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 150
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 200
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support < 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 30 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					check_variable = {
						PER_majlis_support > 250
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 15 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
		clr_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Majlis elections (I.R.)
	id = PER_majlis.29
	title = PER_majlis.29.t
	desc = PER_majlis.29.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Okay
		name = PER_majlis.29.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.29.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
				}
				random_list = {
					35 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.28 #Principalists win
							days = 10
						}
					}
					65 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.27 #Reformists win (more likely to win, as they are not in power)
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
				}
				random_list = {
					65 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.28 #Principalists win (more likely to win, as they are not in power)
							days = 10
						}
					}
					35 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.27 #Reformists win
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
	option = { #Lets pull some strings... (Can help your existing party gain seats)
		name = PER_majlis.29.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.29.b executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_more_likely_win
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_political_power = -250
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					has_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.28 #Principalists win (more likely to win, as they are influenced)
							days = 10
						}
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.27 #Reformists win
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					has_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.27 #Principalists win
							days = 10
						}
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_majlis.28 #Reformists win  (more likely to win, as they are influenced)
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Right-Wing victory
	id = PER_majlis.40
	title = PER_majlis.40.t
	desc = PER_majlis.40.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_controlled_majlis
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_majlis.40.a #Good
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.40.a executed"
		set_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
		clr_country_flag = PER_dissolved_majlis
		if = { #Nationalists fucking hate the left and libtards. Except national front they love them
			limit = {
				OR = {
					western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
					western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_libertarians_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_social_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_communism_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_elections
			set_variable = {
				var = PER_majlis_support
				value = 70
			}
		}
		if = { #Nationalists don't give a shit about everything in between
			limit = {
				OR = {
					neutrality_neutral_muslim_brotherhood_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_autocracy_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_oligarch_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_autocracy_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_reactionaries_are_in_power = yes
					salafist_caliphate_are_in_power = yes
					salafist_kingdom_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_green_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_meh_some_election
			set_variable = {
				var = PER_majlis_support
				value = 120
			}
		}
		#
		if = { #Nationalists fucking love the Shah and other nationalists
			limit = {
				OR = {
					neutrality_neutral_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
					western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
					western_autocrats_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_military_junta_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_fascist_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			set_variable = {
				var = PER_majlis_support
				value = 200
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

				limit = {

country_event = { #The Majlis shifts for alt-history
	id = PER_majlis.50
	title = PER_majlis.50.t
	desc = PER_majlis.50.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_country_flag = PER_majlis_dissolved
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_majlis.50.a #Interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.50.a executed"
		### FLAGS COSMETIC TAG CHANGE
		###
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a liberal majlis, but liberals are not elected, you lose support
				has_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
						western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_libertarians_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a liberal majlis, and liberals are elected, you gain support
				has_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				OR = {
					western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
					western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_libertarians_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
		}
		#######
		if = { #If you have a conservative Majlis, but conservatives are not elected, you lose support
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						neutrality_neutral_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
						western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
						western_autocrats_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
		}
		if = { #If you have a conservative Majlis, and conservatives are in power, you gain support
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				OR = {
					neutrality_neutral_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
					western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
					western_autocrats_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
		}
		#######
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a nationalits Majlis, and nationalists are not elected, you lose support
				has_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_military_junta_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_fascist_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a nationalits Majlis, and nationalists are elected, you gain support
				has_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				OR = {
					nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_military_junta_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_fascist_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
		}
		#######
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a left-wing Majlis, and leftists are not elected, you lose support
				has_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
						emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_social_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_communism_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -30 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If you have a left-wing Majlis, and leftists are elected, you gain support
				has_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				OR = {
					emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_social_are_in_power = yes
					neutrality_neutral_communism_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 40 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

	id = PER_majlis.51
	title = PER_majlis.51.t
	desc = PER_majlis.51.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_country_flag = PER_majlis_dissolved
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
			has_country_flag = PER_freed_majlis
		}
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_majlis.51.a #Interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_majlis.51.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { #If reformists control the majlis, but principalists are elected, then you lose support
				has_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If reformists control the majlis, but reformists are elected, then you gain support
				has_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 50 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { #If Principalists control the majlis, but Reformists are elected, then you lose support
				has_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -50 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { #If Principalists control the majlis, and Principalists are elected, then you gain support
				has_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_gain_some_election
			add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = 50 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

 country_event = {
	id = iran_md.10 # 2003, improving public transport systems
	title = iran_md.10.t
	desc = iran_md.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Yes, let's improve public transportation
		name = iran_md.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.10.a executed"
		one_random_infrastructure = yes
	}
	option = { # No, we can improve internet infrastructure instead
		name = iran_md.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.10.b executed"
		random_core_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = internet_station
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -3.00 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
	}
}

			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}

		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
	}

		PER = {

				emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
			}

			}
			979 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
			}
			408 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
			}
		}

		add_to_variable = { var = PER_pjak_iran_army_size value = 1270 }

		clamp_variable = { var = PER_pjak_strength_var min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				1039 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
				}
			}
			1039 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PER_pjak_activity } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				979 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
				}

#
country_event = {
	id = iran_md.27 # Some time in 2005, PJAK launch attack on mili factory
	title = iran_md.27.t
	desc = iran_md.27.d
	picture = GFX_pjak_event
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		PER = {
			NOT = {
				emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		has_country_flag = PER_pjak_active
		408 = {
			is_controlled_by = PER
		}
	}
	option = { # Damn
		name = iran_md.27.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.27.a executed"
		408 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				damage = 1.0
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	#
	option = { # Damn
		name = iran_md.27.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.27.b executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_pjak_increase_10
		add_to_variable = { var = PER_pjak_strength_var value = 10 }
		clamp_variable = { var = PER_pjak_strength_var min = 0 max = 100 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

#
country_event = {
	id = iran_md.28 # Some time in 2005, PJAK launch attack on mili factory
	title = iran_md.28.t
	desc = iran_md.28.d
	picture = GFX_pjak_event
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		PER = {
			NOT = {
				emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		has_country_flag = PER_pjak_active
		408 = {
			is_controlled_by = PER
		}
	}
	option = { # Damn
		name = iran_md.28.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.28.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			1039 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PER_pjak_activity } }
			979 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PER_pjak_activity } }
			408 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PER_pjak_activity } }
			408 = {
				add_core_of = IKR
			}
			979 = {
				add_core_of = IKR
			}
			1039 = {
				add_core_of = IKR
			}
			408 = {
				remove_core_of = PER
			}
			979 = {
				remove_core_of = PER
			}
			1039 = {
				remove_core_of = PER
			}
			IKR = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = IKR_pjak_state
				set_country_flag = is_IKR_PER
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					408 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
					}
				}
				408 = { transfer_state_to = IKR }
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					979 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
					}
				}
				979 = { transfer_state_to = IKR }
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					1039 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = PER
					}
				}
				1039 = { transfer_state_to = IKR }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}
#
country_event = {
	id = iran_md.29 # State visit to the USA (Pahlavi)
	title = iran_md.29.t
	desc = iran_md.29.d
	picture = GFX_iranian_american_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # Absolutely!
		name = iran_md.29.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.29.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = USA }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = PER }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = iran_md.291
				days = 1
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = PER
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	#
	option = { # No
		name = iran_md.29.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.29.a executed"
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = iran_md.292
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}
#
country_event = {
	id = iran_md.291 # State visit to the USA (Pahlavi)
	title = iran_md.291.t
	desc = iran_md.291.d
	picture = GFX_iranian_american_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # Request investments
		name = iran_md.291.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.291.a executed"
		random_core_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 15.00 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = { # Purchase new aircraft
		name = iran_md.291.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.291.b executed"
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = MR_Fighter3
			amount = 20
			producer = USA
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -37.50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		USA = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 37.50 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = { # Request political support
		name = iran_md.291.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.291.c executed"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

}
### Events to fire once the player takes revolutionary focus
# Organizing the revolutionaries
country_event = {
	id = iran_md.40
	title = iran_md.40.t
	desc = iran_md.40.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#
	option = { # Damn
		name = iran_md.40.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.40.a executed"
		add_political_power = 20
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = iran_md.41
				days = 5
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	#
	option = { # Damn
		name = iran_md.40.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.40.b executed"
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = iran_md.41
				days = 5
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_artesh_5_TT
		set_country_flag = PER_organized_revolutionaries #gives +5% Artesh support on Rev Start
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

	id = iran_md.43
	title = iran_md.43.t
	desc = iran_md.43.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = iran_md.43.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.43.a executed"
		KUR = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = IRQ
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		capital_scope = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name =\"Lwaya Militan KDP\" division_template = \"Lwaya Militan KDP\" start_experience_factor =  1.0"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 8
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = { # No
		name = iran_md.43.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.43.a executed"
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = iran_md.44
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Artesh Declares Neutrality, 1
country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.1
	title = PER_civilwar.1.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # Those bastards
		name = PER_civilwar.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.3.a executed"
		clr_country_flag = PER_starting_the_revolution
		clr_country_flag = PER_starting_the_revolution_2
		set_country_flag = PER_selected_this_focus_already
		hidden_effect = {
			1039 = { transfer_state_to = HRM }
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = HRM
				size = 1.0
				stockpile_ratio = 0
				army_ratio = 1.0
				navy_ratio = 0
				air_ratio = 0
			}
			1039 = { transfer_state_to = PER }
			country_event = {
				id = PER_revolution.10
				days = 4
			}
			# Generals go
			retire_character = PER_mostafa_izadi
			retire_character = PER_mohammad_hejazi
			retire_character = PER_mohammad_jafari
			retire_character = PER_ali_najafi
			retire_character = PER_ahmadreza_pourdastan
			retire_character = PER_ali_hajilo
			retire_character = PER_hassan_saadi
			retire_character = PER_nader_najafi
			retire_character = PER_ahmadreza_pourdastan
			retire_character = PER_qasem_soleimani
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}
# The Civil War, 3
country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.2
	title = PER_civilwar.2.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_iranian_civ_war_country
	option = {
		name = PER_civilwar.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.2.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = PER_interim_government
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PER_american_weapons
				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_revolution.4
					days = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PER_revolutionary_troops
				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_revolution.16
					days = 8
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = PER_persian_revolution
			add_victory_points = {
				province = 10385
				value = 3
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 18 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.35 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.35 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				clear_array = ruling_party
				clear_array = gov_coalition_array
				add_to_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
				update_government_coalition_strength = yes
				set_coalition_drift = yes
				set_ruling_leader = yes
				set_leader = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Revolutionary Council"
				picture = "iranian_juntas.dds"
				ideology = neutral_Social
				traits = {
					stubborn
				}
			}
			#
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = PER
				set_country_flag = PER_mojahded_is_here
				copy_tag = PER
				set_cosmetic_tag = PER_mek_flag
				set_country_flag = is_IRAN
				set_popularities = {
					communism = 100
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					last_election = "1997.6.8"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				start_politics_input = yes
				### Party Popularities
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = 0.00 } #Western_Autocracy
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^1 = 0.00 } #conservatism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = 0.00 } #liberalism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^3 = 0.00 } #socialism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^4 = 0.00 } #Communist-State
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^5 = 1 } #anarchist_communism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.00 } #Conservative
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^7 = 0.00 } #Autocracy
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^8 = 0.00 } #Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih -> Reformists
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^9 = 0.00 } #Vilayat_e_Faqih -> Principalists
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^10 = 0.00 } #Kingdom
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^11 = 0.00 } #Caliphate
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^12 = 0.00 } #Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^13 = 0.00 } #Neutral_Autocracy
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^14 = 0.00 } #Neutral_conservatism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^15 = 0.00 } #oligarchism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^16 = 0.00 } #Neutral_Libertarian
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^17 = 0.00 } #Neutral_green
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^18 = 0.00 } #neutral_Social
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^19 = 0.00 } #Neutral_Communism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^20 = 0.00 } #Nat_Populism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^21 = 0.00 } #Nat_Fascism
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^22 = 0.00 } #Nat_Autocracy
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^23 = 0.00 } #Monarchist
				### Ruling Party
				add_to_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
				startup_politics = yes

				# Leader
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Massoud Rajavi"
					picture = "massoudi.dds"
					ideology = anarchist_communism
					traits = {
						emerging_anarchist_communism
					}
				}

				load_focus_tree = { tree = iran_focus keep_completed = yes }
				set_country_flag = PER_majlis_dissolved
				clr_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_freed_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_controlled_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_dissolved_majlis
			}
			406 = { transfer_state_to = MOJ }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 829 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 3988 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 9816 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 8040 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 10523 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 9074 }
			MOJ = { set_province_controller = 10774 }
			#
			MOJ = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PER
					type = civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = IRI
					type = civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SAZ
					type = civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BLC
					type = civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ARA
					type = civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = IKR
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
			#
			#
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = PER
				set_country_flag = PER_akhoond_flag
				copy_tag = PER
				set_cosmetic_tag = PER_mullahs_government
				set_country_flag = is_IRAN
				retire_country_leader = yes
				set_popularities = {
					communism = 94
					democratic = 6
				}

country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.10
	title = PER_civilwar.10.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # Send the offer
		name = PER_civilwar.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.10.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_MINISTER_GIVEN_AWAY
					has_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = PER_civilwar.16
					}
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = PER_civilwar.17
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PER_MINISTER_GIVEN_AWAY
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_civilwar.16
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_MINISTER_GIVEN_AWAY
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_civilwar.17
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	#
	option = { # Nevermind
		name = PER_civilwar.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.10.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

			factor = 5
		}
	}

# Pezeshkpour
country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.18
	title = PER_civilwar.18.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.18.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # We have no other choice but to accept
		name = PER_civilwar.18.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.18.a executed"
		set_country_flag = PER_PEZESHKPOUR_MAJLIS_CONTROL
		set_country_flag = PER_PEZESHKPOUR_JOINED
		set_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY
		set_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY_PEZESHKPOUR
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_CONCEDE_MAJLIS

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	#
	option = { # Nevermind
		name = PER_civilwar.18.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.18.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

	desc = PER_prime_minister.1.d

		set_country_flag = PER_iranian_minister_given

			factor = 5
		}
	}

# New PM
country_event = {
	id = PER_prime_minister.401
	title = PER_prime_minister.401.t
	desc = PER_prime_minister.401.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = PER_prime_minister.401.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_prime_minister.401.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_iranian_minister_given
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = PER_iranian_minister_given
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_prime_minister.401.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_prime_minister.401.b executed"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PER_iranian_minister_given
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

	title = PER_prime_minister.452.t
	desc = PER_prime_minister.452.d

			var = revolutionary_recovery_status
			value = 10
		}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_prime_minister.452.b

			factor = 5
		}
	}
